            <h2 id="currentFilter_Title">Cocoa Touch Layer</h2>
            <p id="currentFilter_Description" class="visible">
                    


    <title>Cocoa Touch Layer</title>
    <meta id="xcode-display" name="xcode-display" content="render">
    <meta http-equiv="content-type" content="text/html; charset=utf-8">
    <script>
        function listen(elem, evnt, func) {
          if (elem.addEventListener){
            elem.addEventListener(evnt,func,false);
          } else if (elem.attachEvent) {
            var r = elem.attachEvent("on"+evnt, func);
            return r;
          }
        }
        listen(window, 'load', function(evt){ 
          window.location.href = "../index.html#section=Frameworks&topic=Cocoa%20Touch%20Layer";
        });
    </script>

        <a name="//apple_ref/doc/uid/TP40008035" title="Cocoa Touch Layer"></a>Implement a graphical, event-driven application in iOS with the frameworks in the Cocoa Touch Layer. In addition, use the frameworks in this layer to access key device features, such as user contacts. Start your iOS programming at this highest layer, and you'll automatically take advantage of lower-level layers without getting into their details.

</p>
